[browser/base/content/test/browser_bug597218.js]
  1 window(s) [url = chrome://browser/content/tabview.html]
  1 docShell(s)
This isn't intermittent and it's no real leak. browser_bug597218.js is just the first test that causes tabview.html to be loaded.
I know this isn't intermittent, but need to add back the [orange] flags, so post bug 772388, people don't think this is new and file something else. The TBPL posts here might also act as a helpful reminder... ;-)
If I've interpreted bug 753448 correctly, the part 4 patch there should fix this :-)
(In reply to Ed Morley [:edmorley] from comment #3)
> If I've interpreted bug 753448 correctly, the part 4 patch there should fix
> this :-)

Sorry, this will not fix this issue. That's only to avoid introducing a similar issue with the preloaded new tab page. For this bug though, we could so something similar and call TabView.uninit() in the mochitest suite.
